1a1(1): @##// rgya gar skad du/ shrI dz+nyA na tsin+ta tan+t+ra rA dza/ bod skad du/ dpal ye shes bsam pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po// dpal rdo rje sems dpa'al phyag
1a2(1): 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro ma'i 'khor grangs med pa dang / ye shes gsang ba'i gnas na thabs gcig/ 
1a3(1): tu bzhugs pa'i dus su dpa' bo me shes mkha' 'gro zhes bya bas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos gtugs te thal mo sbyar nas gsol pa/ bcom ldan ye shes mnga'/ 
1a4(1): bdag che/ ye shes kyi ni rang bzhin dang / ye shes skye gnas gang dang gang / rgyal po ji ltar legs pa dang / gang la dbang byed gang gis 'dul// de nyid bdag la
1a5(1): bshad du gsol// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ dpa' bo ye shes mkha' 'gro nyon/ ye shes zhes bya rnam pa lnga/ de nyid don la shes pa dang / log
1a6(1): rtog shes pas ma bsgribs phyir/ spyi bo'i ye shes bshad pa'o// me long ye shes mnyam nyid dang / so sor rtog dang byi nan tan// chos dbyings ye shes lnga pa'o// 
1a7(1): de la me long ye shes ni/ dper na g.yang dag me long la/ gzugs brnyan gsal bar snang ba bzhin/ de bzhin sems kyi me long la/ nyon mongs g.ya' ni dag
1a8(1): byas na/ chos rnams gzugs brnyan sgyu mar mthong // sems kyi me long gang yin la/ sgyu ma tsam du snang ba de/ za dad mi byed mnyam sa shes// mnyam
1b1(1): nyid ye shes gang yin pa/ kun rdzob sgyu ma tsam de ni/ las dang mtshan nyid ma 'dres pa/ de nyid so sor rtog ye shes/ de nyid nan tan sgrub byed de/ de nyid don grub
1b2(1): ye shes te/ thams cad chos dbyings gzhan min te/ de phyir chos dbyings ye shes yin/ ye shes skye gnas gang yin pa/ kha sbyar dbus kyi rtsa brgyad do// dbyings
1b3(1): dang ye shes gnyis med tshul/ shar dang lho dang nub dang byang / ye shes bzhi po skye ba'i gnas/ de dag kun 'das lte ba ni/ chos dbyings ye shes skye ba'i gnas// 
1b4(1): me long ye shes mnyam nyid dang // so sor rtog dang bya ba grub/ chos dbyings ye shes la sogs pa/ bdag po byed pa'i phyir dang ni/ zhe sdang dang ni nga rgyal dang / 
1b5(1): 'dod chags dang ni phrag dog dang / de bzhin gti mug la sogs pa'i/ nyon mongs thams cad 'joms pa'i phyir/ rgyal po zhes ni bstan pa yin/ ye shes
1b6(1): mkha' gros yang gsol pa/ byang chub sems ni ji ltar lags/ de nyid dbye ba gang lags dang / de yi gnas dang gzung ba'i gnas/ nges par bzlog/ 
1b7(1): pa'i tshul nyid dang / de nyid kyi ni 'bras bu dang // rtags dang yod tan gang lags pa/ de nyid bdag la bshad du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das kyis
1b8(1): bka' stsal pa/ byang chub sems ni rang rig ste/ dbye ba'i don ni gnyis su bstan/ de yi gnas ni rtsa yin te/ gzung ba rig pa'i 'khor lor te/ 
2a1(1): nges par bzlog pa'i thabs dag ni/ go bzlog pa yi tshul yin no// de nyid 'bras bu gnyis med rtogs// rtags ni
2a2(1): lus la khrag byang dang / bsku langs dang 'dir ba dang / kha zas dang chung lus yang dang // skra dkar gnyer ma dengs pa dang // le lo med dang brtson
2a3(1): 'grus ldan/ de la sogs pa'i rtags rnams 'grub/ de nas yon tan bshad pa ni/ rkeng mgyogs sa steng sa 'og gi/ 'jig rten dngos grub
2a4(1): gang yin dang / 'jig rten las 'dus thob par 'gyur/ gnyis med byang chub sems kyi gnas/ rang rig 'od gsal de nyid do// ye shes rang
2a5(1): bzhin gnas yin te/ rtags ni 'od gsal de nyid do// 'bras bu chos sku 'cheng chen pa'i/ sa ni nges par thob pa'o// rnal 'byor sems
2a6(1): gzung sgom pa brtag/ lus sems tshigs su bcug nas ni/ rang rig sems kyi de nyid la/ de nyid dbyer med bsgom par bya/ de yis thob
2a7(1): me 'bras bu thob/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / ye shes mkha' 'gro la sogs pa'i 'khor thams cad rjes su rang nas/ 
2a8(1): de kho na nyid bla na med pa'i mchod pas mchod de mi snang bar gyur to// dpal 'khor lo sdom pa ye shes bsam pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po rdzogs so// 
2b1(1): piN+Di ta ga yang+ka ra dang / lo tso ba dge slong shAkya shes kyis bsgyur ba/ rgya gang srid du/ 
2b2(1): dzA tan+d+re \u0f7f/ bod skad du/ dpal chags pa'i rgyal po rgyud kyi rgyal po/ dpal rdo rje mkhang grol phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag
2b3(1): gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rje btsun mo'i b+ha ga la
2b4(1): bzhugs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rdo rje snying pos spos dang me tog la sogs pa'i mchod pas mchod nas/ he de dpa'
2b5(1): bo 'jigs pa re/ sems can sangs rgyas rang bzhin na/ mtshan dang dpe byad gang dang gang / stong dang de bzhin rnam thar dang / rdzus
2b6(1): sa mngal skyes sgong skyes dang / drod gabring gnyis gsum bzhi char ci/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ a ni dbu yi gtsug tor
2b7(1): A ni dbu sgra g.yas su 'khyil/ i ni dpral ba'i dbyis mnyam la/ I ni smin mtshams mdzod pu ste/ u ni spyan mig mthon mthong la/ 
2b8(1): ba yi rdzi ma lta bu'o// chu choms bzhi bcu mnga' ba ste/ ror tshems mnyam choms thigs bzang / le la tshoms dkar ro bro mchog/ e ni
3a1(1): 'gram pa seng ge 'dra/ ai ljags shin tu srab pa ste/ oM ni tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang ldan/ oM ni dpung mgo shin tu zlum/ aM ni
3a2(1): bdun mtho ba ru gsungs/ a zhi thal gong rgyas pa ste/ 'di dag bcu drug g.yas bskor ro// de g.yon bskor mtshams nas kyang / a ni pags srab mdog gser
3a3(1): 'dra/ A ni bzhengs bzhin ma btud par/ phyag gnyis pus mor sleb pa'o// i ni ro stod seng ge 'dra// I ni shing n+ya gro lta bur/ chu dang zheng ni gab pa'o// u ni
3a4(1): mdzod spu g.yas su 'khyil/ U ni sku rnams gyen du phyogs// ri mdo mas sba ba skyabs su nub/ rI baR+Sha legs par zlum pa'o// le ni zhabs long tshigs ma mngon// 
3a5(1): l-I ni phyag zhabs 'jam zhing gzhon/ l-I nI phyag mthil zhabs kyi mthil/ 'jam zhing gzhon sha rgyas pa'o// e ni phyag zhabs dra bas 'brel/ ai ni sen mo ring
3a6(1): bste/ oM ni phrug dang nabs mthil la/ 'khor lo dang ni ldan pa yin/ oM ni nabs ni shin tu gnas/ oM na byas rting pa yangs pa ste/ a ni byin pa ri dgas ni/ 
3a7(1): Anal 'i lta bu ste/ skye ban ma shigs snying po ma/ ni pasnyam cu cu gnyis mtshan/ kau ni sen ma zangs mdog 'dra/ kha nis na mo mdog snyam pa/ gan
3a8(1): mamathong / lhan sor ma rnams rnam pa/ nga ni ser mo rnams rgyas pa/ tsa ni sor rnams byin gyis rba/ can rtsa rnams mi mngon pa dzan tsa mdzad
3b1(1): med pa yin/ dz+nyA ni long bu mi mngon pa/ nya ni zhabs mi mnyam pa med/ Ta ni seng ge'i stabs su gshegs/ tA ni glang po'i stabs su gshegs/ DA ni
3b2(1): ngang ba'i stabs su gshegs/ D+ha ni khyu mchog stabs su gshegs/ Na ni g.yas phyogs ldog cing gshegs/ ta ni mdzes par gshegs pa ste/ tha ni mig yo
3b3(1): bar gshegs pa/ da ni sku la 'khril bag chags/ d+ha skra byi dor byas pa 'dra/ ni sku rim par 'tsham pa'o// pa ni skra gtsang ba sku mchog/ bskra rnam par
3b4(1): dag pa'o// b+ha ni mtshan rdzogs ngo bo nyid/ ma skra kho lag yengs shing bzang / ya ni gom pa snyoms pa'o// ra skra shin tu gzhon mdog can/ la ni sgra la 'khrul pa
3b5(1): med/ wa ni sku lus rgyas pa ste/ sha ni byin tu grims pa'o// dza ni yan lag thams cad mdzes/ sa gzigs rab rab med cing dag/ ha dgu zlum pa nyid yin te/ 
3b6(1): k+Sha ni dku skabs byed pa'o// yang kum rnyongs pa yin te/ ra ni phyal phya ma med pa yin/ la ni lte ba zab ste// wa ni lte ba g.yas su 'khyil/ DA ni kun nas mdzes
3b7(1): bI ste/ D+ha nI kun spyod gtsang ma yin/ 'di dag thubs kyi rang bzhin gyis/ g.yas nas bskor ba bzhi bcu yin/ de nas g.yon gyi bzhi bcu yin/ de nas g.yon
3b8(1): gyi bzhi bcu ni/ ni su sde gnag bag med/ kha ni zhing bal ltar 'jam phyag/ ga phyag ri mo mdangs yod pa/ g+ha phyag ri mo zab pa dang / nga phyag ri mo ring ba'o// 
4a1(1): tsan la ha cang mi ring ba/ mnal gzugs kyi gzugs brnyan snang / dzadzA ljags mnyen ljags srab pa// nya ni ljags dmar
4a2(1): ngo bo ste/ glang po'i nga ro 'brug sba Ta/ ni gsung skan mnyen 'jam pa/ DaD+ha mche bzlum dang rnaM/ Na ni mche dkar te tshems mnyam/ tha ni mche ba byin gyis phra/ 
4a3(1): dashangs shin tu mtho ba dang /  shangs shin tu gtsang ba'o// na ni spyan 'od rnam par dag/ pa pha spyan bzung rdzi ma lcug/ ba ni dkar nag bye pad+ma'i/ 'dab ma'i
4a4(1): mdangs 'dra pad+ma'i spyan/ b+ha ni de bzhin smin mtshams ring / ma ya smin mtshams smin skra mnyam/ ra ni de bzhin smin ma snum/ la ni ska ni shal stug cing ring / 
4a5(1): de bzhin wa ni snyan sha la mnyam/ snyan gyi dbang po ma nyams sha/ dpral ba legs par 'byes pa Sha/ sa ni dpral ba'i dbyes che ba/ ha ni dbu dag shin tu rgyas/ 
4a6(1): dbu skra bung ba ltar gnag k+Sha/ dbu skra stug pa ya yin te/ de bzhin dbu skra 'jam par/ dbu skra mi 'dzing ba ni la/ dbu sgra mi gshor ba ni wa/ dbu skra dri zhim
4a7(1): Da yin te/ phyag la dpal gyi be'u dang ni/ bkra shis g.yung drung 'khyil bas brgyan/ sdong ris lta bu rtse yin te/ lte ba sprul pa sring po aM/ gtso bo dpe byed be rgyad cur
4a8(1): ldan/ a ni phyi nang stong pa nyid/ A ni stong pa nyid stong pa/ i ni chen po stong pa nyid/ I ni don dam stong pa nyid/ u ni 'dus byas stong pa nyid/ A ni 'dus ma byas
4b1(1): stong pa/ ri ni mtha' las 'das spyod ba/ rini thog mtha' stong ba nyid/ li ni dor ba med pa stong / lI ni rang bzhin stong pa nyid/ e ni chos rnams thams cad
4b2(1): stong / oM ni rang gi mtshan nyid s+ho/ so ni mi dmigs stong pa nyid/ oM ni dngos po med stong nyid/ oM ni ngo bo stong pa nyid/ dngos med ngo bo nyid aH/ mgrin pa
4b3(1): longs spyod snying po sa/ shes rab stong pa bcu drug rtsa/ gzugs can gzugs rnams la lta ba/ rnam par thar pa dang po a/ nang gzugs med par 'du shes pas/ 
4b4(1): phyi rol gzugs rnams la lta ba/ rnam thar gnyis pa ka yin no// sdug pa rnam par thar pa'i lus/ mngon sum byas nas rdzogs pa ni/ de dag rnam thar gsum
4b5(1): pa tsa/ gzugs kyi 'du shes la 'das pa/ sna tshogs 'du shes yid byed/ nam mkha' mtha' yas la gnas Ta/ nam mkha' mtha' yas las 'das te/ 
4b6(1): nam shes mtha' yas la gnas shing / rnam shes mtha' yas rdzogs pa te/ rnam shes mtha' yas las 'das na/ ci yang med pa la gnas te/ de nyid
4b7(1): rdzogs pa pa yin no// ci yang med pa las 'das te/ 'du shes med min la gnas te/ 'du shes med mir rdzogs pa yang // 'du shes med min las 'das
4b8(1): te/ 'du shes tshor ba 'gog pa'i lus/ mngon sum byas nas rdzogs pa ni/ rnam par thar pa brgyad pas/ snying ka chos kyi 'khor lo hU~M/ gtso bo rnam tha/ 
5a1(1): brgyad dang ldan/ 'di dag rtsa mi rnam par gnas/ 'khor lo'i rgya ni sor gsum ste/ sems can kun la rang bzhin gnas/ 
5a2(1): de phyir sems can sangs rgyas yin/ sna tshogs sdud pa'i mtshan nyid kyang // ring du 'byung zhing zung du gnas/ smin mtshams kyi ni mdzod spu bzhin/ chos
5a3(1): kyi 'byung gnas lte ba la/ g.yas g.yon bu ga lnga lnga ste/ steng 'og kha yis bar nas 'byung / ro ma shar du mngon du phyogs/ brkyang ma nub ste 'og gi
5a4(1): char/ ro mas brkyang ma la 'khyud cing // g.yas pa'i cha ru zung 'jug nyid/ brkyang mas ro ma la 'khyud cing / g.yon gyi cha ru zung 'jug nyid/ g.yas
5a5(1): g.yon rtse mo sgra gsung thugs/ de sgra sngags su rab tu grags/ sngags dang rgyud dang dngos grub sogs/ de nyid las ni byung bas na/ sems can sangs rgyas
5a6(1): rang bzhin no// skye ba bzhi yi rim pa yang / snod bcud ya ba yum la thim ste/ yab yum nyi ma zla bar 'gyur/ snang ba'i thig le yang dag bcas/ 'di dag
5a7(1): nang gi mngal skyes tshul/ A li kA li nyi zla ste/ sems ni thag le'i ngo bor gnas/ nang gi sgong skyes yin par 'dod/ ka dang a las nyi zla ste/ rang
5a8(1): byung thig le drod gsher man/ de dge skad cig rkyen med las/ rang bzhin 'byung ba rdzas skyes sa/ rkyen med sbyor bsgong sogs las/ bde bsde dang
5b1(1): bde ba'i rgyu/ thams cad dran pa gsang ba yi/ mngal na skyes pa'i tshul yin te/ yar la bsreg dang mar lagaso// gnas gsum nyi shu bzhir
5b2(1): 'phro ya/ phyi nang 'dod pa'i mtshan ma yis/ rnga rgyas bde ba ster ba dang / rin po che yi pho brang du/ sems 'dzir gsang ba'i sgong skyes yin/ rang gi
5b3(1): 'dod pa'i mtshon cha yis/ bde ba skye ba drod gshor skyes/ gang gi rkyen gyis ma skyes par/ 'dod nas badre ba'i rgyur skyes la/ bde ba skyes pa rdzus
5b4(1): skyes so// gtum mo go zlog rten gyis sngar/ gtum mo rkyen gyis sbar ba dang / gtum mo rang bzhin sbar ba ni/ mnga' skyes sgong skyes ga sher skyes// 
5b5(1): rdzus skyes rim par sbyar bar bya/ du ma'i gzhi bcas gzhi bcas dang / gzhi med shin tu bzhi med de/ mngal skyes skong skyes drod gsher skyos/ rdzus skyes
5b6(1): bani char rim par sbyaro/ chu dang lam ste 'bras bu kun/ skye ba bzhi yi ngo bor gcig/ dephyir sangs rgyas sems can gnyis/ dngos po ro mnyam gyur pa la/ 
5b7(1): log rtog sgyu mas gnyis smra'akhrul/ rdo rje snying po snying rje che// nang dang gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor yang / nga yis bshad kyis legs par nyon/ sku
5b8(1): yid dkyil 'khor spyi bor sgom/ gsu ni mgrin pa thugs ni zhing / yon tan lte ba 'phrin las ni/ sna rtsed gtubasam par bya/ 'bar ba bani sa la
6a1(1): yang / rdo rje phag mo rab tu grags/ ha ni bde mchog he ru ka/ dpa' bo gcig pa yin par 'dod/ bdun pa dang ni dgu pa/ 
6a2(1): dag/ gsum pa tsU las rab tu grags/ bcu gsum pa dang bco lnga pa/ bcu dgu oM las rab tu grags// nyi shu rtsa lnga nyi shu dgu/ haM gi ngo bor yang dag gnas/ 
6a3(1): sum cu bdun dang drug cu bani/ a yi dkyil 'khor yin par nges/ rtse ni rdo rje phag mo ste/ g.yas g.yon phyag la dbu mnal/ dpa' bo byang chub sems yin te/ 
6a4(1): skye mched bcu gnyis dngas ma yang / bcu gnyis phyag tu rab tu grags/ 'byung bzhi'i dngas ma zhal bzhir nges/ mdzes pa'i phyir na rgyan du bshad/ gsung mchog
6a5(1): bla ma'i zhal nas blang // g.yas g.yon steng 'og sgo bzhi ste// 'dom gang mnyam pa gru bzhi yin/ bdud rtsi lnga ni tshon rtsi lnga/ rtsa ni thig gi rang bzhin te/ ka ba
6a6(1): brgyad ni rkang brgyad do// so sen pa sU tAr sogs/ mkhas pas rtag cing shes par bya/ 'di dag rang bzhin dkyil 'khor te/ dper na rang byung gser dang 'dra/ 
6a7(1): 'di ni bcos ma ma yin te/ rang rig ye shes gzugs brnyan ni/ gzugs brnyan dkyil 'khor sgom pa min/ rdul tshon la sogs bri ba yin/ spos la sogs
6a8(1): pas mchod pa min/ rdo shing lha la phyag mi bya/ rang bzhin gnas pa'i sangs rgyas la/ rang bzhin mchod pas rtag tu mchod/ sku ni dgun dus rang bzhin te// 
6b1(1): 'byung ba'i sku gsum zla ba gsum/ gsung ni dpyid dus ngo bo ste/ 'jug pa'i sku gsum zla ba gsum/ thugs ni dbyar dus ngo bo ste/ gnas pa sku gsum
6b2(1): zla ba gsum/ ye shes ston gyi dus yin te/ sku gsung thugs ni zla ba gsum/ dang po rgyu yis pa yin/ 'khor lo chags pa dmar po la/ yi ge rnams
6b3(1): na dkar pos gas/ lam gyis pa rnam pa gnyis/ ring ba dang ni nye ba'o// de ni 'bras bu'i sa pa yin/ 'khor lo yang dag gnas pa ste/ 'khor long rnam
6b4(1): lha rnams kyang / sku mdog phyag mtshan kun dang bral/ rang bzhin gsal ba dri ma med/ shel ltar gsal ba dri ma med/ mi mthong mthong ba'i ngo bo can/ 
6b5(1): zab cing phra ba'i rang bzhin can/ phyiru sgra mdog phyag mtshan lha/ nA gri shin tu phra ba'i gzugs/ gsang ba'i bde ba lU ru nges/ de las bzlog pa
6b6(1): bzhi pa'i lha/ lus las byung phyir lta zhe'am/ rgyud rnams dag byed phyir na lha/ chags pa'i phyir na lha yin te/ rgyal po shes rab rang bzhin te/ thabs
6b7(1): dang shes rab rang bzhin gyi/ chags pa chen po'i rgyud gsungs so/ de nas sa chen po'ang cher g.yos par gyur te/ mchod pa'i sprin gyi char chen po babs par
6b8(1): gyur to// de nas dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyang rgyud kyi don la dga' zhing mgu ste rjes su yi rang nas mi snang bar gyur to// dpal chags pa'i rgyal po'i
7a1(1): @rgyud kyi rgyal po rdzogs so// rnal 'byor ma tsan+d+ra mA le dang / lo tsa ba dge slong shAkya ye shes kyis
7a2(1): bsgyur ba'o// @##// rgya gar skad du/ sarba ta thA ga ta tsit+ta gar+b+ha ar+tha tan+t+ra/

7a4(1): nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi/ klu gsung thugs kyi rdo rje bdag/ snying po mchog de bzhugs pa'i sku/ rdo rje sem
7a5(1): dpa' la gzigs te/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes sku/ sna tshogs gzugs can sems 'di ni/ mtha' dang bral ba yin mod kyi/ srid dang

7a8(1): khyod kyi gsung / nyid kyis nal nas theg pa shor/ ke ke ru dang margad dang / skrag dang rdo yi snying po dang / rin chen kha dog sna lnga pas/ ye
7b1(1): shes gzhal yas kha dog spras/ nyid las mi gzhan 'jigs byed dang / rgyal sras dang pa gtam nyan dang // 'gro ba 'dul ba'i 'khor rnams so// / 
7b2(1): de nas bcom ldan shA ka thub kyi/ gsung gi dgongs pa mkhyen nas ni/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes kyi/ rang byung ye shes bsdu ba mdzad// 
7b3(1): de bzhin gshegs kyis 'di skad du/ ched du brjod pa rnam par mdzad/ gang zhig rtsol med bde chen don/ lhan cig skyes pa ma mthong na/ sgrub dang / 
7b4(1): rtsol ba ci spyad kyang / byis pa don med ga chad du/ rdzas bzung ba ni 'ching ba nyid/ rten 'brel sgom pa gnyis pa'o// don med nyams myong 'dod pa
7b5(1): yang / 'ching ba'i rgyu ste gsum pa'o/ kha cig e ri'i thal bas byugs/ dbang phyug nam mkha'i rdzas rnams sdud/ 'ching ba'i rgyu ste bzhi pa'o// 
7b6(1): gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// mtha' dang bral ba'i rang bzhin la/ gzung 'dzin nad kyis ci la 'ching / gdong nas dag
7b7(1): pa'i nam mkha' la/ bag chags mtshan mas ci la 'ching / skye 'gag med pa'i chos nyid la/ rgyu 'bras nad kyis ci la 'ching / bsam dang

8a1(1): 'od gsal sna tshogs dus na bde/ rnam dag 'khor lo bde ba la/ bsnun pa'i blo gros log pa yis/ srid
8a2(1): rgyu nges pa'i rtsa bar 'khyams/ gzhan yang ston pas 'di skad gsungs/ zhen chags can gyi gdul bya la/ bde ba chen po bcos ma sbyin/ khong
8a3(1): khro can gyi gdul bya la/ g.yo ba rlung gi bcos ma sbyin/ 'dod pa chu bzhin gdungs pa la/ bkri drang rang rgyud bcos ma sbyin/ kun tu rmongs pa'i
8a4(1): yid can la// stong pa snying rje bcos ma sbyin// ston pas de skad bka' stsal pa/ 'khor rnams bsdu ba rnam mdzad de/ de bzhin gsheg sa la 'di

18b4(1): brjod pa nyid// snying rje med na mi 'grub pas/ de phyir snying rje bskyed par bya/ mtshams med lnga ni byed pa dang / sangs rgyas bstan pa 'khrug byed pa/ zhe sdang rigs kyi ting 'dzin gyis// 
18b5(1): re zhig tsam du gsad par bya/ gzas pa'i sha la rtag tu rol/ kun tu gtum pa'i shugs 'chang ba/ yul dang yul du rol byed pas/ shing rnams la ni gnas nas kyang / dkyil 'khor
18b6(1): zhing rnams skyong bar byed/ nur khrod gnas kyis yongs su bskor/ ma mo'i gnas sogs khyad par byed// klu yis mchod pa'i zhing skyong ba/ me yi phye mas yongasu bskor/ sgo ngang mig gis
18b7(1): khyad par 'gyur/ gtso bo'i sngags kyi lus can te/ sgrub pa po la lus la gnas/ de dag rim par dus bstan pa/ dam tshig ldan pa'i sngags pa yis/ sgrub pa'i rjes rnams khrad pa
18b8(1): las/ 'bru nag gtor ma rab tu shis// sha chen gyis ni brgyan pa yi/ tshogs rdzas b+hA dza gus pas dbul/ phyi nang gsang ba khyad par las/ bstan pa'i tshul gyis 'phrin las las/ 
19a1(1): bye brag rgyan dang gnas skabs pa/ grub dang sgrub pas mngon du 'gyur// dus rnams kun tu zhe sdang gis/ rnam pa kun tu gnom mi bya/ yul min pa la bsad byas na/ 
19a2(1): rnal 'byor dam tshig las nyams phyir/ grub pa nam yang yong mi srid/ khyad par ye shes bla med pa/ dam tshig mgon po sgrub pa yi/ dam tshig 'di ni rmad po che/ bde bar gshegs pa'i lam
19a3(1): sbyor mdzad/ byang chub sems kyi zla ba 'di/ yang ngo mar ngo rab tu gnas/ yar ngo yis ni skyes byed la/ mar ngo la 'grib par byed/ yar ngo yi ni bco lnga la/ byang chub sems kyi mkha'agro yang
19a4(1): bde ba chen por 'dra bar mdzad/ 'di ni nges pa'i don du gsungs/ dkyil 'khor lha nyid lus nyid yin/ gzhan du lha dang dkyil 'khor ni/ btsal yang rnyed par mi 'gyur zhes/ 
19a5(1): 'dren pa dpa' bos rtag tu gsungs/ sku gsung thugs kyi gsang ba la/ drag po kun gyi srog gyur pa/ yon tan 'phrin las dbang phyug gi/ phyi nang gsang ba'i bdag po yin/ ston
19a6(1): pa gnas pa'i rang bzhin las/ 'khor lo dgug bya gnyis med pa stim/ dngas snyigs las ni rgyu 'bras dang // gnas pa khyad par rten 'brel te/ 'khrul dang 'khrul pa ma yin pa/ 
19a7(1): khams gsum kun la dbang byed pas/ 'jig rten las dang ye shes kyi/ mgon po'i khyad par mngon 'byung ba/ gdags pa tha snyad khyab pa po// thun mong bar ni bstan pa yin// 
19a8(1): 'di dag las dang skye bo las/ sgrib pa thun mong lha yin/ dngos dang brgyad pas lung bstan pa/ srog dang srog ma yin pa ste/ rgyu dang rkyen dang bskul ba yis/ gsang sngags
19b1(1): bzlas pa mngon par phye/ 'di ni mngon du 'byung ba'o/ dpal mgon pa chen po dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud las/ gsang ba mngon par 'byung ba'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// 
19b2(1): de nas yang dag bshang bya ba/ he ru ka dpal mgon k+Shi/ gsang ba'i sprul pa nag po che/ 'di yi sgrub rim bshad par bya/ gsang ba'i sgrub pa'i thabs mchog ste/ skal
19b3(1): pa can la sbyin par bya/ gang du sgrub pa'i sa phyogs su/ mi mthun g.yeng ba spang byas nas/ de nas nag po bsgrub par bya/ 'gro ba kun la rab bltas nas/ 
19b4(1): tshad med byang chub sems kyi blos/ snying rje chen po bskyed byas nas/ bde ba'i stan la 'dug nas ni/ lhor bltas skra grol gcer bu yis/ dang por skad cig
19b5(1): tsam gyis ni/ rang lhar bskyed pa'i snying kha ru/ a las zla ba'i dkyil 'khor yang / bsil zhing 'od dang bcas pa bsam/ rang steng raM las nyi dkyil 'khor
19b6(1): rta bdun 'ad zer cha ba dang / me yi rang bzhin 'gro ba bsam/ de 'bras yi ge hU~M nag pa/ ye shes lnga pa'i rang bzhin can/ de yi 'od kyi snang ba las/ dpag
19b7(1): med khe dag pani bcas pasam/ rang bzhin gnas su 'bras pa las/ bram dang ni lhag pa'i g+ha/ dkyil 'khar 'khor lo byangs padang / nag brten pa
19b8(1): 'khor dang bcas/ mdun gyi nam mkhar btsugs pa la/ skabs su 'gro dang mchod pa 'bral/ sdig pa bzhags pa la sogs pa/ bzod par gsol nas gshegs su
21a1(1): dpon du byin gyis brlab bo// de nas ral gri blangs te/ ral gri ming gis dbang bskur bas dbang bskur la/ 'di skad ces chos 'di bshad par bya ste/ ral gri 'di na
21a2(1): rtag bzung la// shes rab rdul 'di dkar smra zhing // nam mkha' sangs rgyas sbyor ba las// 'de bas na myur du 'grub par 'gyur// sangs rgyas bstan pa spang byor dang // sems can mang po bslang ba'i phyir
21a3(1): 'dir bsang sdig par mi 'gyur zhing // bsod nams dag kyang tho bar 'gyur// slob ma rnams la'ang de bzhin shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i dngos grub rnams kyis myur du bla na med pa yang dag
21a4(1): bar rdzogs byang chub mngon par rdzogs 'tshang brgya bar 'gyur ro// chos kyi dkyil 'khor ro// bsgrub pa'ang de bzhin no// ma bsgribs par yang de bzhin du las rnams rngub par 'gyur ba ni// stong pa nyid kyi zhing
21a5(1): nge 'dzin 'thob pa la ni/ thams cad nam mkha' bsgom pas so// mtshan ma med pa'i ting de 'jo'i ba la ni/ mtshan ma dang bral ba'i ting nge 'dzin bsgoms pas so// smon pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin thob pa
21a6(1): la ni/ smon pa med pa bsgoms pas so// rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba chos kyi ye shes thob pa lan/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu bsgoms pas so// nyon mongs pa thams cad gcod pa la ni
21a7(1): chos bsgoms pas so// yi ge thams cad kyi nges tshig gi ye shes la ni/ spros pa med pa'i ye shes bsgoms pas so// gnas thams cad du yi ge chos kyi bya ba mthong ba la naM/ a la so
21a8(1): pa'i yi ga'i ngo bo nyid bsgoms pas so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub thob pa la ni/ rdo rje ral gri'i phyag rgyas so// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i
21b1(1): rgyal po chen po las 'khor lo chen po ltar yi ge bskor ba'i dam tshig ces bya ba/ rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po/ rdzogs so// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams
21b2(1): cad kyi 'khor lo'i nang du 'dus pa'i/ de bzhin gshegs pas yang 'khor la chen po'i 'jug pa zhes bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// rdo rje mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa'i de bzhin
21b3(1): gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor la 'jug par 'gyur ro// don gyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'khor lo la 'jug par 'gyur ro// chos tham
21b4(1): cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni/ dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo la 'jug par 'gyur ro// thams cad mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa ni/ 'khor lo thams cad la 'jug par 'gyur ro// de nas byang chub
21b5(1): sems dpa' sems bskyed ma thag tu/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba nyid kyi don 'di rgya cher ston cing / bzhin rab tu 'dzum pas/ rdo rje 'khor lo thams cad la/ 'jug pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i
21b6(1): snying po 'di smras so// de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po can/ khams gsum du gtogs pa'i sems can dkyil
21b7(1): 'khor du nags nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs las dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi/ dam tshig gi sems dpa' rnams nges par byung nas/ dkyil 'khor gyi ji lta ba bzhin bcugs so//

22a1(1): / 'jug pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i 'khor lo 'i dkyil 'di gsungs so// phyi'i dkyil 'khor ji lta ba bzhin du byas te/ nang gi dkyil 'khor du rdo rje 'khor lo bris la/ 
22a2(1): dbus su rdo rje'i 'khor lo bskor ba bzhag par bya'o// phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' thams cad rnam pa thams cad du/ dkyil 'khor dang po'i tshul du bzhag par bya'o// byi'i 'tshams
22a3(1): rnams su rdo rje'i rigs kyi dkyil 'khor ba ni bri bar bya'o// sgo rnams su mtshan ma rnams sa banag par bya'o// 'di lta ste/ rdo rje sems dpa'i sku dang / rdo rje khro bo'o sku dang / spyan ras gzigs dbang
22a4(1): byug gi sku dang / nam mkha' snying po'i sku rnams so// de nas 'khor lo'i phyag rgya ji lta ba bzhin du/ dkyil 'khor thams cad du sangs rgyas nyid dang / rdo rje 'den pa nyid du 'grub par 'gyur ro// 
22a5(1): de nas 'khor lo blangs la 'khor lo'i ming gi dbang bskur ba blang bar bya zhing / gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor bzhi'i thig btab pa'i rigs rnams la 'jug par bya'o// slob ma bzhug pa yang de bzhin no// 
22a6(1): 'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor ro// bsgrubs pa yang de bzhin no// ma bsgrubs pa yang dkyil 'khor thams cad du 'jug pa la ni rdo rje 'khor lo ste/ rang gi khar bcug la bzhag par bya'o// 
22a7(1): dkyil 'khor chen por 'jug pa la ni/ 'khor lo chen pos so// de bzhin du ngag rgya dkyil 'khor 'jug pa lan/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo'i phyag rgyas so// de bzhin dam tshig gi
22a8(1): dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa la ni/ dam tshig chen po'i 'khor los so// las kyi dkyil 'khor du 'jug pa la ni/ rdo rje thams cad kyi 'khor los so// de bzhin du rdo rje rjes su chags par byang dang / dbang du
22b1(1): du bya ba dang / don thob pa dang / rgyas gdab pa dang / gcad pa dang / 'jug pa dang / mchod pa dang / bdug pa 'dul ba'i las rnams lan/ sems dpa' chen po brgyad kyi phyag rgya g.yon na/ 'khor

22b3(1): de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pa thams cad kyi cho ga rgyas pa snod kyi mchod pa thams cad kyi mchog ces bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// byang chub kyi sems bskyed pa ni de
22b4(1): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su skyob pa nyid ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa'i tshig rgyas pa'o// dam pa'i chos longs
22b5(1): su 'dzin pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'o// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yi ger 'dri ba las dang / yi ger 'drir 'jug pa dang / 'dzin pa dang / klog pa dang /

22b7(1): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nam mkha'i mdzod don de nyid rgya cher ston te/ bzhin rab tu 'dzum zhing las thams cad/ don yod pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i snying lo 'di smras so// /

23a1(1): dpa'i tshul gyis dkyil 'khor chen po'i tshul du bzhugs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' nam mkha'i mdzod/ mchod pa thams cad kyi cho ga rgyas par byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge

23b5(1): gtor ba la ni bzlas pas so// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po las/ sna tshogs rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i/ rtog pa'i rgyal po chen po

23b7(1): ba ye shes snying po nas bya ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// sems can mnyam pa nyid pas khro ba mnyam pa nyid do// sems can thams cad 'dul ba nyid pas
23b8(1): khro ba 'dul ba nyid do// sems can thams cad chos nyid pos khro ba chos nyid do// sems can thams cad rdo rje nyid pas khro ba rdo rje nyid do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad
24a1(1): @'dul ba ni byang chub bo// de nas byang chub sems dpa' bdud kyi stobs kyi thams cad rab tu 'joms pa'i don nyid rgya cher ston te/ bzhin rab tu 'dzum zhing / rdo rje mche
24a2(1): ba'i phyag rgya dang / rdo rje gnod kyi gzugs kyi rdo rjes/ khro bo'i gad mos zhes bya ba'i snying po 'di smras so// hA/ de nas 'di gsungs pa tsam gyis/ gdug pa thams cad 'dul ba'i sem

24b6(1): cad 'dul ba la ni/ rdo rje mche ba'i phyag rgyas so// sems can thams cad 'dul ba la ni/ khro bo ha ha nes rgod cing 'dul bas so// nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi 'dod chags dang bral bas las ltung ba la ni/ 
24b7(1): chos gos snam sbyar gyi sprin sreg gis gos so// dbang bskur ba thams cad dbrog pa la ni/ khams thams cad kyis phye ma'i sbyin sreg gis so// thams cad rgyas gdab pa la ni/ rdo rje khu tshur gyi phyag rgya rgyas so// 
24b8(1): thams cad gcod pa lo ni/ gzugs brnyan byas nas btub pas so// ma rungs pa thams cad dkyil 'khor rnam par gzhig pa la ni// rdo rje gzung nas 'jug par bya'o// mchod pa thams cad rnam
25a1(1): par gzhig pa la ni/ khros nas bzlas brjod bya'o// thams cad bskrad par bya la ni// 'jigs byed kyi lta bas blta bar bya'o// bde ba chen po rdo rje don yod pa'i dam tshig gi rtog
25a2(1): pi rgyal po las/ rdo rje dam tshig ces bya ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po/ rdzogs so// // de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa/ chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la gnas pas/ yang chos
25a3(1): thams cad kyi mchog ces bya ba/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul 'di bshad do// chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mnyam pa nyid do// chos thams cad don nyid pas
25a4(1): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i don nyid do// thams cad chos nyid pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa chos nyid do// thams cad las mnyam pa nyid pas/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mnyam nyid du rig par

266b1(1): bram ze dang ni khyim bdag gcig 'dra 'dangs yin nang // rus pa'i rgyun rnams kyang ni sgyu ma'i nga bzhin te// rdo rje go 'bang de la lan pa'i rang bzhin no// nal
266b2(1): 'byor de la mnyam pa'i ngo bor nges mthong ste// de dang mnyam pa'i rang bzhin sems can rnams la sbas// de yi rnal 'byor rang bzhin lha mos gsungs pa ni// rnam
266b3(1): thams cad der ni gcig pa'i rang bzhin te// gtso bo dang bcas mdzes pa gcig pu 'byung bar 'gyur khyod/ mnyam pa'i rang bzhin de ni sngags pa gcig pu ste// rdo rje rnam pa
266b4(1): spang bar byed pa gcig pu nyid// der ni zhe sdang rang bzhin dag ni zhig pa ste// yan lag byed pa'i chos ni 'byung bar 'gyur ba yin/ der ni rdo rje'i btsun mo gcig rang bzhin/ 
266b5(1): gang tshe rdo rje la ni dbyangs kyis bstod pa'i tshe// lha yi g.yon gyi phyed dang gcig tu gyur par lta// ldang nyid tshad mar byas nas rdo rje sems dpa' de bsgom bya/ gsung gi dkyil
266b6(1): gyi le'u ste gsam pa'o// // glang po dang ni rta dang mi dang khyi dang ni// ba glang sha ste thams cad ma lus gyur pa rnams// dam tshig de nyid gcig/ 
266b7(1): pa'i rang bzhin cad yin te// mkha' mnyam rang bzhin can gyi rnal 'byor pas bza' ba'i/ dam tshig 'di ni lha mo bzhi pos gsungs pa'o// rnal 'byor pa la sgom pa'i
266b8(1): sems dang ldan 'gyur zhing // sems gcig pa ni rdo rje 'chang nyid 'grub 'gyur te// dngos po nyid dang bcas pa'i thugs ni skye bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i dngos
267a1(1): mdzad zhib ma gsungs snying po ste// 'di ltar chos rnams mnyam pa nyid du rtogs bya zhing // de ltar mkha' dang mnyam par
267a2(1): rnam par dpyad par bya// lha 'di rnam snang lnga mo ldarnams de'i bdag nyid// rdo rje theg pa la ni mnyam pa'i rang bzhin te// skul byed mas ni srid pa'i rang bzhin yin
267a3(1): phyir ro// gcig pa'i dang po rdo rje sems te skur mthong ba// rdo rje'i theg par 'dod rnams lha mos 'di skad gsungs// bde ba bskyed pa 'di ni rnam sdang lha mos gsungs// 
267a4(1): 'di ni zla ba'i dbus gnas sgom pa rdo rje'i gsang sngags te/ de ni sems gcig pa yis rdo rje rnam bsgoms pa// rab tu 'bar ba'i rdo rje rtse gsum pa cid do// rnal 'byor gnas
267a5(1): kyi dbus gnas rdo rje'i rang bzhin sgom// ngas ni rdo rje theg par 'di skad du/ chos rnams gcig pa'i rang bzhin nyid du bstan/ sku'i dkyil 'khor gyi le'u se bzhi
267a6(1): pa'o// / dngos mad mi rtag pa las dngos bcas lus sgrom min// lha mos skul ba byed pa'i dngos po ste// de ltar chos las nges par brtags byas pas/ 
267a7(1): sems ni nam mkha' lta bu'i mtshan nyid dang / dngos po theg pa med pa'i dngos por bya// dngos po'i rang bzhin la ni theg pa med pa ste// sems ni nam mkha'
267a8(1): mkha' tshad dang mnyam pa'i rang bzhin can// snga mji bzhin sems ni rnam par sbyar bar bya// ji ltar de ni dngos por bya ba ste// dngos po 'di ni theg par mi
